\"text\": \"The Apache Kafka GroupCoordinator implementation is spread across multiple files in the group-coordinator module and related modules. The core architecture includes:\\n\\n**Main GroupCoordinator Interface and Implementation:**\\nThe GroupCoordinator interface (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java) defines the contract for group coordination operations. The primary implementation is GroupCoordinatorService (GroupCoordinatorService.java), which implements the GroupCoordinator interface and delegates to GroupCoordinatorShard for request handling. The GroupCoordinatorShard class (GroupCoordinatorShard.java) is the actual shard-level coordinator that handles individual requests and delegates to GroupMetadataManager for business logic.\\n\\n**Group Metadata State Machine:**\\nThe GroupMetadataManager (GroupMetadataManager.java) is the core state machine manager that handles all group metadata operations. It manages three types of consumer groups:\\n\\n1. **Classic Groups** - Implement the original Kafka consumer group protocol:\\n   - ClassicGroup.java: Main group class managing classic groups with states (EMPTY, PREPARING_REBALANCE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, STABLE, DEAD)\\n   - ClassicGroupState.java: Enum defining the five group states with valid state transitions\\n   - ClassicGroupMember.java: Represents a member in a classic group\\n\\n2. **Modern Consumer Groups** - Implement the new consumer group protocol:\\n   - ConsumerGroup.java: Modern consumer group implementation\\n   - ConsumerGroupMember.java: Modern consumer group member\\n   - CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java: Builds current assignment for modern groups\\n\\n3. **Share Groups** - For shared consumption:\\n   - ShareGroup.java: Share group implementation\\n   - ShareGroupMember.java: Share group member\\n   - ShareGroupConfig.java: Share group configuration\\n   - ShareGroupAssignmentBuilder.java: Assignment builder for share groups\\n\\n4. **Streams Groups** - For Kafka Streams applications:\\n   - StreamsGroup.java: Streams group implementation\\n   - StreamsGroupMember.java: Streams group member\\n   - StreamsGroupHeartbeatResult.java: Heartbeat result wrapper\\n\\n**JoinGroup and SyncGroup Request Handlers:**\\nThe request handlers are implemented in multiple layers:\\n- KafkaApis.scala (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/KafkaApis.scala) contains handleJoinGroupRequest and handleSyncGroupRequest which route to the group coordinator\\n- GroupCoordinatorService.java implements the public joinGroup and syncGroup methods\\n- GroupCoordinatorShard.java has joinGroup and syncGroup request handlers\\n- GroupMetadataManager.java contains the main business logic:\\n  - classicGroupJoin: Handles classic group join requests\\n  - classicGroupSync: Handles classic group sync requests\\n  - consumerGroupJoin: Handles modern consumer group join\\n\\n**Heartbeat Expiry Detection and Member Management:**\\nHeartbeat handling is implemented across multiple request handlers and internal mechanisms:\\n- handleHeartbeatRequest in KafkaApis.scala: Routes classic group heartbeats\\n- handleConsumerGroupHeartbeat in KafkaApis.scala: Routes modern consumer group heartbeats\\n- handleShareGroupHeartbeat in KafkaApis.scala: Routes share group heartbeats\\n- handleStreamsGroupHeartbeat in KafkaApis.scala: Routes streams group heartbeats\\n- classicGroupHeartbeat in GroupMetadataManager.java: Main heartbeat handler for classic groups\\n- consumerGroupHeartbeat in GroupMetadataManager.java: Heartbeat handler for modern consumer groups\\n- shareGroupHeartbeat in GroupMetadataManager.java: Heartbeat handler for share groups\\n- streamsGroupHeartbeat in GroupMetadataManager.java: Heartbeat handler for streams groups\\n- rescheduleClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat in GroupMetadataManager.java: Manages heartbeat expiry deadlines for classic group members\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure:**\\n- GroupCoordinatorConfig.java: Configuration for the group coordinator including timeouts and intervals\\n- GroupCoordinatorRecordSerde.java and GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.java: Serialization and helper utilities\\n- OffsetMetadataManager.java: Manages offset metadata and expiration\\n- GroupConfigManager.java: Manages group-level configurations\\n- GroupCoordinatorMetrics.java: Metrics tracking for group states and operations\\n\\n**State Enum Classes:**\\n- ClassicGroupState.java (both in group-coordinator and clients modules): Defines the five classic group states (EMPTY, PREPARING_REBALANCE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, STABLE, DEAD) with state transition validation\\n- ConsumerGroupState.java: State enum for modern consumer groups\\n- GroupState.java: Abstract state representation\\n\\nThe state machine enforces transitions between states, with ClassicGroupState defining valid previous states for each state transition. Members are managed through member-specific heartbeat scheduling and timeout detection, which triggers member removal and potential group state changes.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":7539,"cache_read_input_tokens":81130,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":7539},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"8a0c31bc-70e8-4c30-8287-392dccbe7310","uuid":"2919af2d-043f-4382-b48e-4f45f8e9d8b3"}
